efx,efy,efz,ega,egf,efn=egd(efu:sub(1,2),16),egd(efu:sub(3,4),16),egd(efu:sub(5,6),16),egd(efu:sub(7,8),16),egd(efu:sub(9,10),16),{}for egg=0,egf-1 do efn[efu:sub(11+egg,11+egg)]=egg end local efo,efs,eft,kk,gi,efv="",{},0,efx,0,95 while efv<#efu do local lo=efn[efu:sub(efv,efv)]or 0 local hi=efn[efu:sub(efv+1,efv+1)]or 0 local egi=lo+hi*egf eft=eft+1;efs[eft]=efq(efr(efr(egi,efz),kk)%256)kk=(kk*efy+gi+ega)%256;gi=gi+1;efv=efv+2 if eft>=256 then efo=efo..egb(efs);efs={};eft=0 end end if eft>0 then efo=efo..egb(efs)end local egh,egj=nil,64 if egj==64 then local a,b=(loadstring or load)(efo);if a then egh=a else warn("[PVM] "..tostring(b))end;egj=146 end local egk if egj==146 then if egh then egk=egh end;egj=161 end if egj==161 and egk then return egk(...)end end)()
